***раз.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a> (74)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Inherited from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_East_Slavic" class="extiw" title="w:Old East Slavic">Old East Slavic</a></span> <i class="Cyrs mention" lang="orv">разъ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="orv-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razŭ</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">strike</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Cognate to <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разить.html>рази́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:резать.html>ре́зать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">rézatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raz</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́за</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>разы́</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><strong class="selflink"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></strong></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>time <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">an instance or occurrence</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́за</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">dva <b>ráza</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">twice</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:еще.html>ещё</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ješčó <b>raz</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">once more; one more time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:ни.html>ни</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>ра́зу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ni <b>rázu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">not once; never</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">ne <b>raz</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">repeatedly</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:как.html>как</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">kak <b>raz</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">just; just in time</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>one <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">in counting</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a> ... <a href = vnd.unilang:марш.html>марш</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raz</b>, dva, tri ... marš!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one, two, three ... go!</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:два.html>два</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:три.html>три</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:огонь.html>ого́нь</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>raz</b>, dva, tri, ogónʹ!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one, two, three, fire!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_2">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raz</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> once, one day, once upon a time
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Я</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:видеть.html>ви́дел</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:она.html>её</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:веселый.html>весёлом</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вихрь.html>ви́хре</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:бал.html>ба́ла</a>…</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Ja vídel <b>raz</b> jejó v vesjólom víxre bála…</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I saw her once in the merry whirlwind of a ball… (M. Yu. Lermontov, Verse 145)</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Conjunction">Conjunction</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">raz</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> if, since; as long as
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:садиться.html>сади́сь</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>раз</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:прийти.html>пришёл</a>.</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Sadísʹ, <b>raz</b> prišól.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Sit down, as long as you’ve come.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:раз.html>Раз</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:он.html>он</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сказать.html>сказа́л</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:значить.html>зна́чит</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:так.html>так</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:и.html>и</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:быть.html>бу́дет</a>!</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Raz</b> on tak skazál, znáčit, tak i búdet!</i> ― <span class="e-translation">Since he said so, this is how it’s going to be!</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разбег.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́г</a> (14153)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́г</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbég</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́га</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́ги</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́гов</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>running start
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыжок.html>прыжо́к</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́гу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">pryžók s <b>razbégu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">running jump</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́г</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:при.html>при</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:взлет.html>взлёте</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razbég</b> pri vzljóte</i> ― <span class="e-translation">takeoff run</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:прыгать.html>пры́гать</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́гу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">prýgatʹ s <b>razbégu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">take a running jump</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:нырять.html>ныря́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:с.html>с</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́гу</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">nyrjátʹ s <b>razbégu</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">take a running dive</span></div></dd>

<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:здесь.html>здесь</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:нет.html>нет</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:для.html>для</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́га</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">zdesʹ net mesta dlja <b>razbéga</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is no room to take one's run</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разбегавшийся.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбегавшийся.html>разбегавшийся</a> (9958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбегавшийся.html>разбега́вшийся</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbegávšijsja</span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">past active imperfective participle of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбегаться.html>разбега́ться</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbegátʹsja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбегаться.html>разбега́ться</a> (9958)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-а́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-átʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбегаться.html>разбега́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbegátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбежаться.html>разбежа́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to scatter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбегаться.html>разбега́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razbegátʹsja</b> po mestám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run to one's places/posts/stations</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:глаз.html>глаза́</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбегаться.html>разбега́ются</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:у.html>у</a> кого́-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">glazá <b>razbegájutsja</b> u kovó-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">one doesn't know where to look first</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take a run, to run up <i>(before jumping, diving, etc)</i></li></ol>

<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбег.html>разбе́г</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razbég</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разбега́ние</span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razbegánije</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бегать.html>бе́гать</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bégatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбегаться.html>разбе́гаться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbégatʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start running strenuously</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to start running and not stop</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бежать.html>бежа́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bežátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбежаться.html>разбежа́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbežátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбегаться.html>разбега́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to scatter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбежаться.html>разбежа́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:место.html>места́м</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razbežátʹsja</b> po mestám</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to run to one's places/posts/stations</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to take a run, to run up <i>(before jumping, diving, etc)</i>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:негде.html>не́где</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбежаться.html>разбежа́ться</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">négde <b>razbežátʹsja</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">there is no room for a running jump (dive, etc.)</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***разбивать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбивать.html>разбива́ть</a> (10761)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ва́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-vátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбивать.html>разбива́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbivátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to crash, to crush, to smash, to shatter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбивать.html>разбива́ть</a> чьи́-либо. <a href = vnd.unilang:аргумент.html>аргуме́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razbivátʹ čʹí-libo. arguménty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to demolish someone's arguments</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбивать.html>разбива́ть</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдребезги.html>вдре́безги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razbivátʹ vdrébezgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock to pieces, to smash into smithereens, to shatter, to make matchwood of something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to defeat, to beat, to smash
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбивать.html>разбива́ть</a> наголову</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">razbivátʹ nagolovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to crush., to wipe out</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to divide, to break/down)</li>
<li>to lay out <i>(park)</i>, to mark out</li>
<li>to pitch <i>(a tent)</i>, to set up <i>(a tent or a camp)</i></li>
<li><i>a body part</i> to knock, to hurt badly, to break, to fracture, to damage severely</li>
<li><i>polygraphy</i> to space out</li></ol>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбитый.html>разби́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razbítyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***разбиваться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбиваться.html>разбива́ться</a> (12696)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбивать.html>разбива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбиваться.html>разбива́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbivátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбиться.html>разби́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break, to crash, to shatter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break up, to split, to divide</li>
<li>to collapse, to die (e.g. of dreams)</li>
<li>to get seriously hurt</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбивать.html>разбива́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbivátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***разбирать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбирать.html>разбира́ть</a> (4839)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-бира́ть</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-birátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбирать.html>разбира́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbirátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разобрать.html>разобра́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to dismantle, to disassemble, to take apart, to deconstruct</li>
<li>to analyse, to parse</li></ol>

<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбирать.html>разбира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбираться.html>разбира́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbirátʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разобраться.html>разобра́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to deal with, to sort out
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:я.html>Мне</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:лень.html>лень</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбираться.html>разбира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:со.html>со</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:сломанный.html>сло́манным</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:окно.html>окно́м</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">Mne lenʹ <b>razbirátʹsja</b> so slómannym oknóm.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">I'm too lazy to deal with the broken window.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to see into, to comprehend, to work with
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбираться.html>разбира́ться</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ракета.html>раке́тах</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:не.html>не</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:легко.html>легко́</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:надо.html>на́до</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:физика.html>фи́зику</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:понимать.html>понима́ть</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Razbirátʹsja</b> v rakétax ne lexkó — nádo fíziku ponimátʹ.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation">Working with rockets isn't easy — you need to understand physics.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to figure out, to work out</li>
<li>to sort out</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбирать.html>разбира́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbirátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбитый.html>разби́тый</a> (2296)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Participle">Participle</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***разбить.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a> (3728)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:бить.html>бить</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">bitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbítʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбивать.html>разбива́ть</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to break, to crash, to crush, to smash, to shatter
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></b> чью́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:жизнь.html>жизнь</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razbítʹ</b> čʹjú-libo žiznʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to ruin someone's life</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></b> чьи́-либо <a href = vnd.unilang:аргумент.html>аргуме́нты</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razbítʹ</b> čʹí-libo arguménty</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to demolish someone's arguments</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:вдребезги.html>вдре́безги</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razbítʹ</b> vdrébezgi</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to knock to pieces, to smash into smithereens, to shatter, to make matchwood of something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to defeat, to beat, to smash
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></b> на́голову</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razbítʹ</b> nágolovu</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to crush, to wipe out, to rout</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to divide, to break down</li>
<li>to lay out (park), to mark out</li>
<li>to pitch (a tent), to set up (a tent or a camp)</li>
<li>to knock, to hurt badly, to break, to fracture, to damage severely (a body part)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">polygraphy</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to space out</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">billiard</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to make the first shot</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбитной.html>разбитно́й</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razbitnoj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбитый.html>разби́тый</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razbítyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***разбиться.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбиться.html>разби́ться</a> (6060)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ся</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-sja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбиться.html>разби́ться</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbítʹsja</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбиваться.html>разбива́ться</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break, to crash, to shatter</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to break up, to split, to divide</li>
<li>to collapse, to die (e.g. of dreams)</li>
<li>to get seriously hurt</li>
<li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">passive of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбить.html>разби́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbítʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></span></span></li></ol>

***разбой.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́й</a> (16705)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́й</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbój</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́я</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́и</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́ев</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>robbery, brigandage
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:морской.html>морско́й</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́й</a></b></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn">morskój <b>razbój</b></i> ― <span class="e-translation">piracy</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́й</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:большой.html>большо́й</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:дорога.html>доро́ге</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>razbój</b> na bolʹšój doróge</i> ― <span class="e-translation">highway <b>robbery</b></span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">law</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> armed robbery, aggravated robbery <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">robbery with the threat or use of dangerous or deadly force</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">billiards</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> break shot</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>In modern legal usage, <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> is distinguished from <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:грабеж.html>грабёж</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">grabjóž</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (robbery with the use of non-dangerous force).</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбойник.html>разбо́йник</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razbójnik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбойный.html>разбо́йный</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">razbojnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li>

***разбойник.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разбойник.html>разбо́йник</a> (4298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбой.html>разбо́й</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">razbój</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ник</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-nik</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбойник.html>разбо́йник</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbójnik</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr> <abbr title="animate">anim</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбойник.html>разбо́йника</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбойник.html>разбо́йники</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разбойник.html>разбо́йников</a></b>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разбо́йница</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>brigand, robber</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> rogue, wretch</li></ol>

<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разболтать.html>разбо́лтанный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razbóltannyj</span>) (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)разбо́лтаннее</b> <i>or</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">(<a href = vnd.unilang:по.html>по</a>)разбо́лтанней</b>)

***разболтать.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:разболтать.html>разболта́ть</a> (17107)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">раз-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">raz-</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:болтать.html>болта́ть</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">boltátʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:разболтать.html>разболта́ть</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">razboltátʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> (<i>imperfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru">разба́лтывать</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to reveal, to give away (a secret)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to shake up, to mix, to stir</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">colloquial</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to loosen</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
